                               <h3 class="Uo8X3b OhScic zsYMMe">
                                Description
                               </h3>
                               <span>
                                Jos Alberto "Pepe" Mujica Cordano is a Uruguayan politician, former Revolutionary and farmer who served as the 40th President of Uruguay from 2010 to 2015. A former guerrilla with the Tupamaros, he was tortured and imprisoned for 14 years during the military dictatorship in the 1970s and 1980s.
                               </span>
